808 forever!! Love that he's staying local, he's someone who I never followed because I lived 10 minutes from him so it felt creepy especially after seeing him in his Jeep (he publicly shared his car type back then) picking up Zippy's right in front of me as I'm picking up Zippy's. I have so much respect for him seeing how he's made his home an ode to Hawaii but also Polynesian/Pacific Islander and Asian cultures and it's done in a way that feels respectful and appreciative, it's not at all over the top/performative and cheap. Many who live in Hawaii usually fall into three camps, 1-you connect with Aina, Mauka, Makai, and Aloha (land, mountain, ocean, warmth/love/fellowship/peace) on a deep level that makes you feel like you've never seen or felt anything more beautiful and know that this is a paradise and want to take it all in, learn about it all, and really become local (different than being Hawaiian/PI) and truly appreciate the give and take of living somewhere like Hawaii, 2-you think Hawaii is nice and enjoy it, you buy the art and local created items and learn a few words and traditions but it's just a beautiful place to visit until you are back on mainland where you flex that you've lived there and use it as some way to claim your "cultured", 3- you hate it, you hate the food, culture, weather, isolation (can't just travel off the island at your whim, there's traffic, only so many flights, can only drive so far and it's never fast), the various weather that can be storming on the Windward side (east side of Oahu) and beautifully sunny on the Leeward side (west side of Oahu), and either think it's great for vacation but terrible to live there or think it's terrible for vacation and to live there. Hawaii makes you realize you can't hide from yourself, you can't just driveway to another state or get on an international flight to anywhere you want, and that you have to have patience because majority of everything is shipped in and there's literally only so much to go around so you can't be selfish and expect to have your Amazon prime order in two days (it takes average 7-10 days). Hawaii is home, my husband is from there and we've lived there for many years together and truly love it but that doesn't mean it's a flawless paradise; the homeless community is only growing more and more, home prices are forcing locals to have multiple generations in small houses/apartments (3 generations in 800sqft is normal), the school systems are some of the worst in the nation, and way too many of the government leaders are more concerned with their own benefits than what's best for Hawaii (railway on Oahu is a glaring example). My husband and I bought house and sold it 3 years later almost to the day and sold it for a price we cant afford to pay, we literally can't buy a house we owned for 3 years because values are so high (Airbnb is a huge part of this, people came in to buy vacation homes and rent them out on Airbnb even though it's illegal but the local and state government doesn't do anything because it benefits them in a lot of ways).  All that to say that seeing Brentman stay in Hawaii, honoring Hawaii, and truly loving Hawaii is such a huge way to show his character, he could move to LA and live that perfected fake lifestyle that so many fall for but he stayed true to himself and stayed in Hawaii. Much respect! ğŸ’œğŸ¤™
